We’ve created detailed sports betting guides to teach bettors what they need to know in plain English, including betting odds and lines.</p>

<p>Now that you understand what Odds Scanner US offers, let’s switch gears and discuss two of the most critical concepts in sports betting: odds and lines. Understanding these concepts will impact how successful you’ll be in the long term.</p>
<h3>Sports Betting Odds Explained</h3>
<p>Understanding sports betting odds is the first step to making more money from betting. Odds show how much a bookmaker will pay when you win a bet. They represent the probability of a particular outcome.</p>
<p>Bookmakers provide pre-match odds for those who want to place bets before games start as well as live betting odds for those who wish to wager as games unfold. Different sportsbooks determine their odds in different ways, so the odds for a single match often vary across sports betting websites.</p>
<p>Odds Scanner US helps punters bet on the most valuable betting odds today by comparing offers from various bookies.</p>
<h3>Why Should You Care About Betting Odds?</h3>
<p>When you wager on the best odds, you&#8217;re guaranteed a better return if you win your bet. If you don&#8217;t use the most valuable sports betting odds, you lose money even when you win.</p>
<p>For example, let’s look at the recent MLS game between Charlotte and Los Angeles. Here are the odds from two bookmakers:</p>
<ul>
<li>Bookmaker 1: 2.80 (1) 3.30 (X) 2.45 (2)</li>
<li>Bookmaker 2: 2.80 (1) 3.45 (x) 2.49 (2)</li>
</ul>
<p>The game ended as 0-1. If you’d staked $100 on Los Angeles Galaxy with bookmaker 1, you could have won $245. If you placed the same bet with bookmaker 2, you could have won $249.</p>
<h3>Sports Betting Lines Explained</h3>
<p>A betting line is a kind of wager where the bookmaker sets a number to handicap a particular team. This gives both teams an equal chance of “winning.” The handicap created also ensures only two outcomes.</p>
<p>For instance, let’s say the Cleveland Cavaliers are playing the Toronto Raptors. If a bookmaker deems the Cleveland Cavaliers to have a 20-point advantage, they can handicap the Cavs by 20 points. This means that if the Cavs only win by 15 points, a bet on the Raptors will pay (and a bet on the Cavs will not).  Odds Scanner US helps you get the best betting lines today, including live betting lines.</p>
<h3>Why Care About Betting Lines?</h3>
<p>Understanding sports betting lines helps you to identify the best betting opportunities. You get a comprehensive outlook of betting and figure out whether to bet on moneylines, point spreads, totals, or futures. To bet successfully, you need to know how betting lines work.</p>
<p>Choosing the best betting lines can be a great determiner of how much money you make from a wager. At Odds Scanner US, we provide the best sports betting lines today as provided by the top sportsbooks in the country.</p>

Our top-notch tools will help you do your simulations so that you only place the most valuable bets.</p>

</div></div></article><div class="content__inner__content__faq"><h2 id="faqs-about-odds-scanner-us-amp-sports-betting">FAQs About Odds Scanner US &amp; Sports Betting</h2><div class="content__inner__content__faq--subtitle"><p>Check out the Odds Scanner US FAQ section for answers to some of your most pressing questions.</p>
</div><div class="accordion"><div class="accordion__items"><div class="accordion__items__item"><button class="accordion__items__item__title"><h3>How do you read betting odds?</h3><div class="accordion__items__item__title--icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path stroke="#0F9960" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9 5 5 1 1 5"></path></svg></div></button><div class="accordion__items__item__text"><p>The most popular odds in the US are moneyline odds denoted by a positive or negative sign. For instance, the Pittsburgh Steelers playing the Kansas City Chiefs has the following odds:</p>
<p>Steelers: +585</p>
<p>Chiefs: -760</p>
<p>You’ll need to risk 100 on the Steelers for a potential win of $585. You need to bet $760 to win $100 if you decide to go with the Chiefs.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion__items__item"><button class="accordion__items__item__title"><h3>What does the +/- mean in betting odds?</h3><div class="accordion__items__item__title--icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path stroke="#0F9960" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9 5 5 1 1 5"></path></svg></div></button><div class="accordion__items__item__text"><p>The minus (-) indicates the team favored to win, while the plus (+) indicates the underdog. In points spread betting, the minus sign indicates that a certain number of points will be deducted from the final score. Conversely, the + indicates that the same points will be added to the other team’s final score.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion__items__item"><button class="accordion__items__item__title"><h3>How are betting odds calculated?</h3><div class="accordion__items__item__title--icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path stroke="#0F9960" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9 5 5 1 1 5"></path></svg></div></button><div class="accordion__items__item__text"><p>Odds calculation is a complex process. Oddsmakers calculate odds by compiling data and doing a comprehensive analysis to ensure that they get near-perfect results. They consider all factors, including previous records, injuries, fatigue, current form, and more.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion__items__item"><button class="accordion__items__item__title"><h3>How do money lines work?</h3><div class="accordion__items__item__title--icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path stroke="#0F9960" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9 5 5 1 1 5"></path></svg></div></button><div class="accordion__items__item__text"><p>Money lines involve wagering on one of the three possible match outcomes. Players predict whether a game will end as a home win, a draw, or an away win.</p>
</div></div><div class="accordion__items__item"><button class="accordion__items__item__title"><h3>What is spread betting?</h3><div class="accordion__items__item__title--icon"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 10 6"><path stroke="#0F9960" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="1.5" d="M9 5 5 1 1 5"></path></svg></div></button><div class="accordion__items__item__text"><p>Sportsbooks set a spread to even the odds between two unevenly matched teams. For instance, if the Washington Commanders are a -3 point favorite when playing the Kansas City Chiefs, the spread is -3 points. If you bet on the Washington Commanders, they must win by at least three points.</p>
